# Germans demand we order the SS to stop touting their 2nd amendment rights or something
country_event = {
	id = BRG.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event BRG.1"}
	title = BRG.1.t
	desc = BRG.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event13

	trigger = {
		tag = BRG
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #agree
		name = BRG.1.a
		GER = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = reich.18 }
			clr_country_flag = SS_partisans
		}
		add_political_power = -25
	}
	option = { #'agree'
		name = BRG.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		GER = { country_event = { days = 1 id = reich.18 } }
		add_political_power = -25
	}
	option = { #lol nah fam
		name = BRG.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		GER = { country_event = { days = 1 id = reich.19 } }
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}

# We win!
country_event = {
	id = BRG.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event BRG.7"}
	title = BRG.7.t
	desc = BRG.7.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event4

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			BRG = {
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = -10
					name = threat.21.t
				}
			}
			TNO_World_Tension_subtract_10 = yes
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #take the land
		name = BRG.7.a
		add_political_power = 100
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		clr_country_flag = fra-brg_war
		FRA = {
			clr_country_flag = fra-brg_war
			remove_ideas = FRA_the_treaty_of_vichi
			transfer_state = 23
			transfer_state = 19
			transfer_state = 25
			transfer_state = 26
			transfer_state = 31
			transfer_state = 22
			transfer_state = 21
		}
		BRG = {
			transfer_state = 792
			transfer_state = 787
			transfer_state = 786
			transfer_state = 791
			transfer_state = 24
			transfer_state = 33
			transfer_state = 789
			transfer_state = 790
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = BRT
			}
			BRT = {
				transfer_state = 747
				transfer_state = 30
			}
			set_province_name = {
				id = 11535
				name = "Can"
			}
			set_province_name = {
				id = 6449
				name = "Cherbour"
			}
			set_province_name = {
				id = 9478
				name = "Añje"
			}
			747 = { set_state_name = "Briovera" }
			30 = { set_state_name = "Liger" }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					country_exists = BRT
				}
			}
			BRG = {
				transfer_state = 747
				transfer_state = 30
				transfer_state = 14
			}
			set_province_name = {
				id = 11535
				name = "Kän"
			}
			set_province_name = {
				id = 6449
				name = "Coriallo"
			}
			set_province_name = {
				id = 9478
				name = "Andekaver"
			}
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 3509
			name = "Mannzeller"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 9732
			name = "Stefanstadt"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 11611
			name = "Burgen"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 9507
			name = "Neustadt"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 512
			name = "Aurelstadt"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 13365
			name = "Piktenstadt"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 3671
			name = "Turon"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 620
			name = "Limogen"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 3549
			name = "Eburo"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 3594
			name = "Vichusstadt"
		}
		set_province_name = {
			id = 9523
			name = "Westen-Paris"
		}
		BRG_Domestic_GUI_Add_France = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = BRG_unlock.4 days = 10 } }
	}
	#option = { #kep it going!
		#	name = BRG.7.b
		#	add_political_power = -100

country_event = { #Heydrich has failed us
	id = BRG.9
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event BRG.9"}
	title = BRG.9.t
	desc = BRG.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event4

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = BRG.9.a
		unlock_national_focus = BRG_a_predictable_failure
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRG_idea_advisors }
			remove_ideas = BRG_idea_advisors
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRG_idea_support_personnel }
			remove_ideas = BRG_idea_support_personnel
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BRG_idea_special_forces }
			remove_ideas = BRG_idea_special_forces
		}
		TNO_BRG_main_tree_swap = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Globalplan Supply Penalty
	id = BRG.100
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event BRG.100"}
	title = BRG.100.t
	desc = BRG.100.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = BRG.100.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRG_anger_charlemagne
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRG_anger_langemarck
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRG_anger_wallon
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = FRA
					NOT = {
						state = 204 #Ost Paris
						state = 786 #West Paris
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 140 } }
					add_to_variable = { CharlemagneSupport = 8 }
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { CharlemagneSupport = 12 }
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 6 #Flandern
						state = 34 #Wallonien
						state = 29 #Pickardien
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state = 6 }
					add_to_variable = { LangemarckSupport = 16 }
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { LangemarckSupport = 6 }
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 6 #Flandern
						state = 34 #Wallonien
						state = 29 #Pickardien
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state = 16 }
					add_to_variable = { WalloonSupport = 16 }
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { WalloonSupport = 6 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event3

		tag = BRG
		#has_completed_focus = BRG_the_breton_contact
		BRT = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = BRG_focus.829.a
	}
}

country_event = { #Iberia notified one of their terorrists just got stronger
	id = BRG_kondor.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event BRG_kondor.4"}
	title = BRG_kondor.4.t
	desc = {
		text = BRG_kondor.4.desc.cnt
		trigger = { BRG = { has_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_cnt } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = BRG_kondor.4.desc.fslp
		trigger = { BRG = { has_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_fslp } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = BRG_kondor.4.desc.tba
		trigger = { BRG = { has_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_tba } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = BRG_kondor.4.desc.eta
		trigger = { BRG = { has_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_eta } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event13

	option = {
		name = BRG_kondor.4.a
		if = {
			limit = { BRG = { has_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_cnt } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_add_cnt_supplies_small_tt
			add_to_variable = { IBR_CNT_Resources = 1 }
			clr_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_cnt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { BRG = { has_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_fslp } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_add_fslp_supplies_small_tt
			add_to_variable = { IBR_FSLP_Resources = 1 }
			clr_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_fslp
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { BRG = { has_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_tba } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_add_tba_supplies_small_tt
			add_to_variable = { IBR_TBA_Resources = 1.5 } #More affected due to being puppets
			clr_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_tba
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { BRG = { has_country_flag = BRG_smuggled_to_eta } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_add_eta_supplies_small_tt
			add_to_variable = { IBR_ETA_Resources = 1 }
			clr_country_flag =  BRG_smuggled_to_eta
		}
	}
}

				limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 140 } }
				subtract_from_variable = { HimmlerSupport = 4 }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		if = { limit = { NOR = { has_cosmetic_tag = NOR_GER } }
			country_event = { id = BRG_infra.21 days = 4 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOR = { has_government = fascism }
					NOR = { has_government = national_socialism  }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = BRG_infra.26 days = 4  }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = BRG_infra.29 days = 4  }
		}
 	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event burgundy_political.14" }
	title = burgundy_political.14.t
	desc = burgundy_political.14.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event12

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = burgundy_political.14.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		BRG_Domestic_GUI_Decrease_Walloon_Loyalty = yes
		subtract_from_variable = {
			BRG_Walloon_Mod_Base_Loyalty = 0.003
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Raiding Walloon
	id = burgundy_political.19
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event burgundy_political.19" }
	title = burgundy_political.19.t
	desc = burgundy_political.19.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event10

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = burgundy_political.19.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect =  {
			set_temp_variable = { BRG_failure_risk = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { BRG_failure_risk = BRG_walloon_prep }
			random_list = { #Success rtate based on amount of prep
				BRG_charlemagne_prep = { country_event = { id = burgundy_political.20 days = 3 } }
				BRG_failure_risk = { country_event = { id = burgundy_political.21 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Walloon dead
	id = burgundy_political.20
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event burgundy_political.20" }
	title = burgundy_political.20.t
	desc = burgundy_political.20.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event3

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Happy HImmler
		name = burgundy_political.20.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRG_killing_walloon
		hidden_effect =  {
			set_country_flag = BRG_walloon_dead
			clr_country_flag = BRG_selected_operation
			if = { #Start Charlemagne with higher sus
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = BRG_charlemagne_dead } }
				multiply_variable = { BRG_charlemagne_legion_sus = 1.5 }
			}
			every_owned_state = { set_variable = { WalloonSupport = 0 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Walloon Alive
	id = burgundy_political.21
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event burgundy_political.21" }
	title = burgundy_political.21.t
	desc = burgundy_political.21.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event11

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Fuck
		name = burgundy_political.21.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRG_walloon_failure
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = BRG_selected_operation
			clr_country_flag = BRG_pursuing_walloon
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = Walloon_Loyal }
				clr_country_flag = Walloon_Loyal
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = Walloon_Obedient }
				clr_country_flag = Walloon_Obedient
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = Walloon_Questionable }
				clr_country_flag = Walloon_Questionable
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = Walloon_Disloyal }
				clr_country_flag = Walloon_Disloyal
			}
			set_country_flag = Walloon_Revolting
		}
	}
}

				set_variable = { BRG_Conversion_Susceptibility = 24 }
				set_variable = { HimmlerSupport = 60 }
				set_variable = { CharlemagneSupport = 30 }
			}
			787 = {
				set_variable = { BRG_Conversion_Susceptibility = 35 }
				set_variable = { HimmlerSupport = 60 }
				set_variable = { CharlemagneSupport = 30 }
			}
			24 = {
				set_variable = { BRG_Conversion_Susceptibility = 60 }
				set_variable = { HimmlerSupport = 60 }
				set_variable = { CharlemagneSupport = 30 }
			}
			33 = {
				set_variable = { BRG_Conversion_Susceptibility = 56 }
				set_variable = { HimmlerSupport = 60 }
				set_variable = { CharlemagneSupport = 30 }
			}
			790 = {
				set_variable = { BRG_Conversion_Susceptibility = 53 }
				set_variable = { HimmlerSupport = 60 }
				set_variable = { CharlemagneSupport = 30 }
			}
			792 = {
				set_variable = { BRG_Conversion_Susceptibility = 60 }
				set_variable = { HimmlerSupport = 60 }
				set_variable = { CharlemagneSupport = 30 }
			}
			set_variable = { BRG_National_Indoctrination = 50 }
		}
		TNO_BRG_domestic_tree_swap = yes
	}
}
country_event = { #Unlocks famine tree phase 1
	id = BRG_unlock.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event BRG_unlock.8" }
	title = BRG_unlock.8.t
	desc = BRG_unlock.8.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event13

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = BRG_unlock.8.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRG_unlock_famine_foci
		set_country_flag = BRG_Famine_Begun
		set_country_flag = BRG_agriculture_phase_1
		TNO_BRG_domestic_tree_swap = yes
		set_variable = { BRG_famine_stop_progress = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event deciding whether famine fires early or not
	id = BRG_unlock.100
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event BRG_unlock.100"
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { BRG_Rodomo_Cost > 1399 } }
			country_event = { id = BRG_unlock.8 days = 8 }
		}
		else = { country_event = { id = BRG_unlock.8 days = 373 } }
	}
	title = BRG_unlock.100.t
	desc = BRG_unlock.100.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRG_fuckyoutex_event14

	hidden = yes #Player should never see this
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
}
